1. 為什麼稱為「中國大歷史」？
   - Translation: Why is it called "The Great History of China"?
   - Grammar Structure: Interrogative sentence
   - Important Words:
     - 為什麼 (wai4 sam6): why
     - 稱為 (cing1 wai4): called
     - 中國 (zung1 gwok3): China
     - 大歷史 (daai6 lik6 si2): great history

2. 第一章　西安與黃土地帶
   - Translation: Chapter One: Xi'an and the Loess Plateau
   - Grammar Structure: Noun phrase
   - Important Words:
     - 第一章 (dai6 jat1 zoeng1): chapter one
     - 西安 (sai1 on1): Xi'an
     - 與 (jyu4): and
     - 黃土地帶 (wong4 tou2 dei6 daai3): loess plateau

3. 第二章　亞聖與始皇
   - Translation: Chapter Two: Ya Sheng and the First Emperor
   - Grammar Structure: Noun phrase
   - Important Words:
     - 第二章 (dai6 ji6 zoeng1): chapter two
     - 亞聖 (aa3 sing3): Ya Sheng
     - 與 (jyu4): and
     - 始皇 (ci2 wong4): first emperor

4. 第三章　土壤、風向和雨量
   - Translation: Chapter Three: Soil, Wind Direction, and Rainfall
   - Grammar Structure: Noun phrase
   - Important Words:
     - 第三章 (dai6 saam1 zoeng1): chapter three
     - 土壤 (tou2 joeng6): soil
     - 風向 (fung1 hoeng3): wind direction
     - 和 (wo4): and
     - 雨量 (jyu5 loeng6): rainfall

5. 第四章　兵馬俑的幕後
   - Translation: Chapter Four: Behind the Terracotta Warriors
   - Grammar Structure: Noun phrase
   - Important Words:
     - 第四章 (dai6 sei3 zoeng1): chapter four
     - 兵馬俑 (bing1 maa5 jung2): terracotta warriors
     - 的 (dik1): of
     - 幕後 (mok6 hau6): behind the scenes

6. 第五章　第一帝國：樹立楷模
   - Translation: Chapter Five: The First Empire: Setting a Model
   - Grammar Structure: Noun phrase
   - Important Words:
     - 第五章 (dai6 ng5 zoeng1): chapter five
     - 第一帝國 (dai6 jat1 dai3 gwok3): the first empire
     - 樹立 (syu6 lap6): set up
     - 楷模 (kai3 mou4): model1. Sentence: 第六章　名士成為軍閥
   Translation: Chapter 6: The Scholar Becomes a Warlord
   Grammar Structure: This sentence is a simple structure, with "第六章" (Chapter 6) as the subject and "名士成為軍閥" (The Scholar Becomes a Warlord) as the predicate.
   Important Words:
   - 第六章 (dai6 luk6 zoeng1): Chapter 6
   - 名士 (ming4 si6): scholar
   - 成為 (sing4 wai4): become
   - 軍閥 (gwan1 faat3): warlord

5. Sentence: 第十章　第二帝國：已有突破，但未竟事功
   Translation: Chapter 10: The Second Empire: There Has Been a Breakthrough, But the Task is Not Yet Complete
   Grammar Structure: This sentence is a compound sentence, with "第十章" (Chapter 10) and "第二帝國" (The Second Empire) as the subjects and "已有突破，但未竟事功" (There Has Been a Breakthrough, But the Task is Not Yet Complete) as the predicates.
   Important Words:
   - 第十章 (dai6 sap6 zoeng1): Chapter 10
   - 第二 (dai6 ji6): second
   - 帝國 (dai3 gwok3): empire
   - 已有 (ji5 jau5): already have
   - 突破 (dat6 po4): breakthrough
   - 但 (daan6): but
   - 未 (mei6): not yet
   - 竟 (ging2): end
   - 事功 (si6 gung1): task1. 第十一章　北宋：大膽的試驗
   Translation: Chapter 11 - Northern Song: A Bold Experiment
   Grammar Structure: The sentence is a simple structure, with the chapter number (第十一章) followed by the topic of the chapter (北宋：大膽的試驗).
   Important Words:
   - 第十一章: Chapter 11 (dai6 sap6 jat1 zoeng1)
   - 北宋: Northern Song (bak1 sung4)
   - 大膽的試驗: A bold experiment (daai6 daam2 dik1 si3 jim6)

   - 國家: Nation (gwok3 gaa1)

5. 第十五章　晚明：一個停滯但注重內省的時代
   Translation: Chapter 15 - Late Ming: A Stagnant but Introspective Era

   - 但: but (daan6)
   - 注重: Emphasize (zyu3 zung6)
   - 內省: Introspective (noi6 sing2)
   - 的: of (dik1)
   - 時代: Era (si4 doi6)1. Sentence: 第十六章　滿洲人的作為

2. Sentence: 為什麼稱為「中國大歷史」？
   Translation: Why is it called "Chinese Macro-history"?
   Grammar Structure: This is an interrogative sentence. It starts with the question word "為什麼" (why), followed by the verb "稱為" (is called) and the object "中國大歷史" (Chinese Macro-history).
   Important Words: 
   - 為什麼 (wai4 sam6): why
   - 稱為 (cing1 wai4): is called
   - 中國大歷史 (zung1 gwok3 daai6 lik6 si2): Chinese Macro-history

3. Sentence: ──中文版自序
   Translation: --- Preface of the Chinese version
   Grammar Structure: This sentence is a noun phrase, consisting of a dash and two nouns.
   Important Words: 
   - 中文版 (zung1 man4 baan2): Chinese version
   - 自序 (zi6 ci4): preface

4. Sentence: macro-history這名詞刻下看來由我創用。
   Translation: The term "macro-history" seems to have been coined by me.
   Grammar Structure: This is a declarative sentence. It starts with the subject "macro-history這名詞" (the term "macro-history"), followed by the verb "看來" (seems) and the object "由我創用" (have been coined by me).
   Important Words: 
   - macro-history: macro-history
   - 這名詞 (ze5 ming4 ci4): this term
   - 刻下 (hak1 haa6): now
   - 看來 (hon3 loi4): seems
   - 由我創用 (jau4 ngo5 cong3 jung6): have been coined by me1. 如果有前人用過，則恕我查訪未周。
   Translation: If it has been used by predecessors, then forgive me for my incomplete investigation.
   Grammar Structure: Conditional sentence (如果...則...) with the main clause expressing a polite request for forgiveness.
   Important Words:
   - 如果 (yu4 gwo2): if
   - 前人 (cin4 jan4): predecessor
   - 用過 (jung6 gwo3): used before
   - 恕我 (so2 ngo5): forgive me
   - 查訪 (caa4 fong2): investigate
   - 未周 (mei6 zau1): not thorough, incomplete

2. 其實此間之出處與是非已無關宏旨，因為這名詞縱是新穎，已乏創意。
   Translation: In fact, the origin of this term is irrelevant to the grand purpose, because even though this term is novel, it lacks creativity.
   Grammar Structure: Compound sentence with two clauses connected by 因為 (because).
   Important Words:
   - 其實 (kei4 sat6): in fact
   - 此間 (ci2 gaan1): this
   - 出處 (ceot1 cyu3): origin
   - 是非 (si6 fei1): right and wrong
   - 無關 (mou4 gwaan1): irrelevant
   - 宏旨 (wang4 zi2): grand purpose
   - 名詞 (ming4 ci4): term
   - 新穎 (san1 jing6): novel
   - 創意 (cung4 ji3): creativity

3. 經濟學家以貨幣之流通影響到物質與雇傭之最基本的原則統稱之為「宏觀經濟學」（macroeconomics）。
   Translation: Economists call the basic principle that the circulation of money affects material and employment "macroeconomics".
   Grammar Structure: Complex sentence with a relative clause modifying the main clause.
   Important Words:
   - 經濟學家 (ging1 zai3 hok6 gaa1): economist
   - 貨幣 (fo3 bai6): money
   - 流通 (lau4 tung1): circulation
   - 影響 (jing2 hoeng2): affect
   - 物質 (mat6 zat1): material
   - 雇傭 (gu3 jung4): employment
   - 原則 (jyun4 zek3): principle
   - 宏觀經濟學 (wang4 gun1 ging1 zai3 hok6): macroeconomics

4. 而以內部較精密之觀察有如涉及物價指數與商業週期等詳情稱為「微視經濟學」（microeconomics）由來已久。
   Translation: And the detailed observation of internal intricacies such as price indices and business cycles is long known as "microeconomics".
   Grammar Structure: Compound sentence with two clauses connected by 而 (and).
   Important Words:
   - 內部 (noi6 bou6): internal
   - 精密 (zing1 mat6): intricate
   - 觀察 (gun1 caat3): observation
   - 物價指數 (mat6 gaa3 zi2 sou3): price index
   - 商業週期 (soeng1 jip6 zau1 kei4): business cycle
   - 微視經濟學 (mei4 si6 ging1 zai3 hok6): microeconomics
   - 由來已久 (jau4 loi4 ji5 gau2): long known1. 亦從未有人出面自稱為始作俑者。
   Translation: There has never been anyone who came forward and claimed to be the originator.
   Grammar Structure: Subject + Time + Negative Verb + Object
   Important Words:
     - 亦 (jik6): also, too
     - 從未 (cung4 mei6): never
     - 有人 (jau5 jan4): someone
     - 出面 (ceot1 min6): come forward
     - 自稱 (zi6 cing1): claim oneself as
     - 始作俑者 (ci2 zok3 jung2 ze2): the originator

2. 宏觀與微觀亦不過放寬視界與計及精微之不同。
   Translation: Macro and micro are nothing more than the difference between broadening the field of vision and taking into account the minutiae.
   Grammar Structure: Subject + Negative Verb + Object + Conjunction + Object
   Important Words:
     - 宏觀 (wang4 gun1): macro
     - 與 (jyu6): and
     - 微觀 (mei4 gun1): micro
     - 不過 (bat1 gwo3): nothing more than
     - 放寬 (fong3 fun1): broaden
     - 視界 (si6 gaai3): field of vision
     - 計及 (gai3 kap6): take into account
     - 精微 (zing1 mei4): minutiae
     - 不同 (bat1 tung4): difference

3. 改稱大小，轉用於歷史，顯係模仿而非發明。
   Translation: Renamed as big and small, used in history, it is obviously imitation rather than invention.
   Grammar Structure: Verb + Object + Conjunction + Verb + Object + Adjective
   Important Words:
     - 改稱 (goi2 cing1): renamed as
     - 大小 (daai6 siu2): big and small
     - 轉用 (zyun2 jung6): used in
     - 歷史 (lik6 si2): history
     - 顯係 (hin2 hai6): obviously is
     - 模仿 (mou4 fong3): imitation
     - 而非 (ji4 fei1): rather than
     - 發明 (faat3 ming4): invention

4. 至於我自己將宏觀及放寬視野這一觀念導引到中國歷史研究裡去，倒確經過一段長期間的周折。
   Translation: As for myself, I have indeed gone through a long period of twists and turns to bring the concept of macro and broadening the field of view into Chinese historical research.
   Grammar Structure: Preposition + Subject + Verb + Object + Time + Adverb + Verb + Object
   Important Words:
     - 至於 (zi3 jyu1): as for
     - 我自己 (ngo5 zi6 gei2): myself
     - 將 (zoeng1): will
     - 宏觀 (wang4 gun1): macro
     - 及 (kap6): and
     - 放寬 (fong3 fun1): broaden
     - 視野 (si6 je5): field of view
     - 觀念 (gun1 nim6): concept
     - 導引 (dou6 jan5): guide
     - 中國 (zung1 gwok3): China
     - 歷史 (lik6 si2): history
     - 研究 (jin4 gau3): research
     - 倒確 (dou2 kok3): indeed
     - 經過 (ging1 gwo3): go through
     - 一段長期間 (jat1 dyun6 coeng4 kei4 gaan1): a long period of
     - 周折 (zau1 zit3): twists and turns1. 大部原因出自命運之安排。
   Translation: The main reason comes from the arrangement of fate.
   Grammar Structure: Subject + Verb + Object
   Key Words:
   - 大部 (daai6 bou6) - major part
   - 原因 (jyun4 jan1) - reason
   - 出自 (ceot1 zi6) - comes from
   - 命運 (ming6 wan6) - fate
   - 安排 (on1 paai4) - arrangement

2. 我年輕時從軍十年。
   Translation: I served in the army for ten years when I was young.
   Grammar Structure: Subject + Time + Verb + Duration
   Key Words:
   - 我 (ngo5) - I
   - 年輕時 (nin4 hing1 si4) - when young
   - 從軍 (cung4 gwan1) - served in the army
   - 十年 (sap6 nin4) - ten years

3. 解甲退伍之後，負笈於海外，可謂「學書未成先習劍，用劍無功再讀書」。
   Translation: After demobilization, I studied abroad, which can be described as "learning to write before learning to use a sword, and reading again after failing to use a sword".
   Grammar Structure: Time + Condition, Action, Result
   Key Words:
   - 解甲退伍 (gai2 gaap3 teoi3 mou5) - demobilization
   - 負笈於海外 (fu6 kap1 jyu1 hoi2 ngoi6) - studied abroad
   - 學書 (hok6 syu1) - learning to write
   - 未成 (mei6 sing4) - before completion
   - 先習劍 (sin1 zaap6 gim3) - first learn the sword
   - 用劍無功 (jung6 gim3 mou4 gung1) - use the sword without success
   - 再讀書 (zoi3 duk6 syu1) - read again

4. 有了這樣一段顛簸之經驗。
   Translation: I have had such a bumpy experience.
   Grammar Structure: Subject + Verb + Object
   Key Words:
   - 有了 (jau5 liu5) - have had
   - 這樣 (ze2 joeng6) - such
   - 一段 (jat1 dyun6) - a period of
   - 顛簸 (din1 but6) - bumpy
   - 經驗 (ging1 jim6) - experience
1. 自己尚在憧憬於近身所見聞的事蹟之真意義
   - Translation: I am still longing for the true meaning of what I have seen and heard.
   - Grammar Structure: Subject + Verb + Object. The subject is "自己" (myself), the verb is "尚在憧憬於" (still longing for), and the object is "近身所見聞的事蹟之真意義" (the true meaning of what I have seen and heard).
   - Important Words: 自己 (myself, zi6 gei2), 尚 (still, soeng4), 憧憬 (longing for, cung1 ging2), 近身 (close to, gan6 san1), 所見聞 (what I have seen and heard, so2 gin3 man4), 事蹟 (events, si6 zik6), 真意義 (true meaning, zan1 ji3 jik6)

2. 而一旦授有學位，作為人師，在美國學子之前講解中國歷史，深覺得不能照教科書朗誦

Grammar structure: This sentence is a complex sentence with multiple clauses. It starts with the time adverb "後來" (later), followed by the subject "《明代十六世紀之財政與稅收》書成" (the book "Financial and Taxation of the Ming Dynasty in the 16th Century" was completed). The final clause "不得已也" (which was inevitable) serves as the conclusion of the sentence.

- 不得已 (bat1 dak1 ji5): inevitable

   - 千差 (cin1 caa1): thousands of differences.1. Sentence: 因為如此，全朝代避免整體的改組而能支持二百七十六年。
   Translation: Because of this, the entire dynasty was able to support itself for 276 years by avoiding overall reorganization.
   Grammar Structure: The sentence starts with the conjunction "因為" (because) followed by "如此" (this), indicating the reason for the following action. The main body of the sentence is "全朝代避免整體的改組而能支持二百七十六年", which is a complex sentence structure with "避免整體的改組" (avoiding overall reorganization) being the method and "能支持二百七十六年" (was able to support itself for 276 years) being the result.
   Vocabulary:

   Translation: However, such central control produces a negative effect: this system does not encourage local development of its strengths, but creates an artificial balance.
   Grammar Structure: The sentence starts with "但是" (however) indicating a contrast to the previous sentence. "如此之中央管制產生一種負面作用" is the main clause, with "此體系不鼓勵各地發展其特長，而製造一種人為的平衡" being an explanation of the negative effect.

Grammar Structure: This sentence is a complex sentence. It starts with a conjunction "而" (and), followed by a phrase "由上至下以泥土敲打而成的梯級" (the steps made by striking the earth from top to bottom), then uses a particle "則" to indicate the consequence, and ends with the main clause "顯示出殯時必有繁縟之儀節" (show that there must be elaborate rituals at the funeral).

Important Words:
- 梯級 (Steps): tai1 kap1

3. 周朝的制度，向稱「封建」，英文總是譯為feudal，其實封建制度與歐洲的feudalism（封建制度）只有某些方面相似，而且其相似處在精神方面，而不一定在實質。

Translation: The system of the Zhou Dynasty is often called "feudalism", and it is always translated into English as feudal. In fact, the feudal system is only similar to European feudalism in some respects, and its similarities are more spiritual than substantial.

Grammar Structure: Subject (周朝的制度) + Verb (向稱) + Object (「封建」) + Additional Information (英文總是譯為feudal) + Conjunction (其實) + Subject (封建制度與歐洲的feudalism) + Verb (只有某些方面相似) + Additional Information (而且其相似處在精神方面，而不一定在實質).

Important Words:
- 周朝 (jāu1 chìuh4): Zhou Dynasty
- 制度 (jai3 douh6): system
- 向稱 (heung3 chīng1): often called
- 英文 (yīng1 màhn4): English
- 總是 (júng2 sī1): always
- 譯為 (yihk6 wàih4): translated as
- 其實 (kèih4 saht6): in fact
- 歐洲 (āu1 jāu1): Europe
- 只有 (jí2 yáuh5): only have
- 某些方面 (máuh5 sē1 fōng1 mihn6): some aspects
- 相似 (sēung1 chíh5): similar
- 精神方面 (jīng1 sàhn4 fōng1 mihn6): spiritual aspect
- 不一定 (bāt1 yāt1 díng6): not necessarily
- 實質 (saht6 jāt1): substantial1. 大致說來兩方都是以世襲貴族掌握地方政府。

3. 而尤其是進入戰國這一段歷史上號稱「百家爭鳴」的時代，各種政治哲學興起，既富有內容，又多品目，茲後二千年的中國歷史中再也無此精到之處。

3. 道家對世俗的權威無好感，認為「聖人不死，大盜不止」。
   Translation: Taoists have no fondness for worldly authority, believing that "the sage does not die, the great thief does not stop".
   Grammar Structure: Subject + Predicate + Object + Complement, where the subject is "道家" (Taoists), the predicate is "對世俗的權威無好感" (have no fondness for worldly authority), and the complement is "認為「聖人不死，大盜不止」" (believing that "the sage does not die, the great thief does not stop").

4. 他們崇信宇宙間的一元組織，願意回歸到原始的簡樸，抵抗各種侵害自由的措施，不管其為威迫或是利誘。
   Translation: They revere the cosmic unity, wish to return to the original simplicity, resist all measures that infringe upon freedom, regardless of whether they are threats or temptations.

Sentence 1: 通常他們支持獨裁者，以賞罰為不二要義心目中的法律則不外軍法和戒嚴法。

Grammar Structure: The sentence is a complex sentence with three clauses. The main clause is "他們支持獨裁者", followed by two subordinate clauses "以賞罰為不二要義" and "而這些獨裁者心目中的法律則不外軍法和戒嚴法".

2. 雖說在某一地各年的雨量可以相差極大，但是全中國的平均雨量卻有定型。

   Translation: Although the annual rainfall in a certain place can vary greatly, the average rainfall across China has a pattern.

   Grammar structure: Although...But.... The first part "雖說在某一地各年的雨量可以相差極大" (Although the annual rainfall in a certain place can vary greatly) is a concession clause, and the second part "但是全中國的平均雨量卻有定型" (But the average rainfall across China has a pattern) is the main clause.

   Important words:
   - 雖說 (seoi1 jyut6): although
   - 某一地 (mau5 jat1 dei6): a certain place
   - 各年 (gok3 nin4): each year
   - 雨量 (jyu5 loeng6): rainfall
   - 可以 (ho2 ji5): can
   - 相差 (soeng1 caa1): differ
   - 極大 (gik6 daai6): greatly
   - 但是 (daan6 si6): but
   - 全中國 (cyun4 zung1 gwok3): all over China
   - 平均 (ping4 gwan1): average
   - 定型 (ding6 jing4): pattern

3. 這現象不難解釋，帶著濕氣的熱風，愈吹入內地，被蒸發的程度也愈為增高。

   Translation: This phenomenon is not difficult to explain, the hot wind carrying moisture, the more it blows into the inland, the higher the degree of evaporation.

   Grammar structure: Subject + Verb + Object. The subject is "這現象" (This phenomenon), the verb is "不難解釋" (is not difficult to explain), and the object is "帶著濕氣的熱風，愈吹入內地，被蒸發的程度也愈為增高" (the hot wind carrying moisture, the more it blows into the inland, the higher the degree of evaporation).

   Important words:
   - 這現象 (ze5 jin6 zoeng6): this phenomenon
   - 不難 (bat1 naan4): not difficult
   - 解釋 (gaai2 sik1): explain
   - 帶著 (daai3 zoek6): carrying
   - 濕氣 (sap1 hei3): moisture
   - 熱風 (jit6 fung1): hot wind
   - 愈 (jyu6): more
   - 吹入 (ceoi1 jap6): blow into
   - 內地 (noi6 dei6): inland
   - 被蒸發 (bei6 zing1 faat3): be evaporated
   - 程度 (cing4 dou6): degree
   - 增高 (zang1 gou1): increase1. Sentence: 而且沿海下雨就已減少了空中的濕氣。
   Translation: Moreover, the rainfall along the coast has already reduced the humidity in the air.
   Grammar Structure: The sentence starts with "而且" (moreover) to connect with the previous context. "沿海下雨" (the rainfall along the coast) is the subject, "已" (already) is an adverb indicating the action has been completed, "減少" (reduced) is the verb, and "空中的濕氣" (the humidity in the air) is the object.
   Important Words:
   - 而且 (ji4 ke4): moreover
   - 沿海 (jin4 hoi2): along the coast
   - 下雨 (ha6 jyu5): rain
   - 已 (ji5): already
   - 減少 (gaam2 siu2): reduce
   - 空中 (hung1 zung1): in the air
   - 濕氣 (sap1 hei3): humidity

2. Sentence: 此中值得注意的是所謂「十五吋等雨線」。
   Translation: What is worth noting here is the so-called "fifteen-inch isohyet".
   Grammar Structure: "此中" (here) is the topic, "值得注意的" (what is worth noting) is the relative clause modifying the topic, "是" (is) is the linking verb, and "所謂「十五吋等雨線」" (the so-called "fifteen-inch isohyet") is the complement.

   - 所謂 (so2 wai6): so-called

Translation: The system of Qin has become streamlined, and the thoughts of Legalism constitute its ideology. Although it stands on the position that human nature is evil, it also believes that humanity can collectively be good.

3. 史書中提及他有一次因風受阻而不能渡湘水，歸罪湘君女神作祟，於是遣發三千囚徒，去砍伐山上的樹木以資報復，可見得他在和超自然的力量作對，而不是震惑於超自然的力量。

Grammar Structure: This sentence is a compound-complex sentence. It starts with a time clause (組織新政權時), followed by two coordinated clauses (既不能追隨舊世族的蹤跡，也無須憑藉他們大張旗鼓) expressing negation.
Important Words:
- 組織 (zou2 zik6): organize
- 新政權 (san1 zing3 kyun4): new regime
- 追隨 (zeoi1 ceoi4): follow
- 舊世族 (gau6 sai3 zuk6): old clans
- 蹤跡 (zung1 zik1): traces
- 大張旗鼓 (daai6 zoeng1 kei4 gu2): grandiose

Sentence 3: 這可不是說中國社會革命的條件業已成熟，即使幾千年後中國也還沒有樹立一種民主體制。
Translation: This is not to say that the conditions for the Chinese social revolution have matured, even if China has not established a democratic system even after thousands of years.
Grammar Structure: This sentence is a compound-complex sentence. It starts with a negative declarative clause (這可不是說中國社會革命的條件業已成熟), followed by a concessive clause (即使幾千年後中國也還沒有樹立一種民主體制).
Important Words:
- 中國 (zung1 gwok3): China
- 社會革命 (se5 wui6 gaak3 ming6): social revolution
- 條件 (tiu4 gin6): conditions
- 成熟 (sing4 suk6): mature
- 幾千年後 (gei2 cin1 nin4 hau6): thousands of years later

Translation: It is even more out of the question to accurately represent the vast and evenly distributed rural grassroots organizations at this time.

Grammar Structure: Subject + Verb + Object. The subject is omitted in the sentence, but it can be inferred from context. The verb is "能夠確切的代表" (can accurately represent), and the object is "龐大而又均勻的農村基層組織" (vast and evenly distributed rural grassroots organizations). "在這時候更不足論" means "even more out of the question at this time".

Translation: The first major problem encountered by the new dynasty is that the empire is too vast.

   - 草原地帶 (cao3 yuan2 di4 dai4): Grassland area.1. 到了公元前五十五年，匈奴分裂為五部自相征伐。

3. 【外戚專權】

Translation: [The power of the maternal relatives]

Grammar Structure: Topic

Important Words:
- 外戚 (ngoi6 cik1): maternal relatives
- 專權 (zyun1 kyun4): power1. 可是在這些軍事行動中已產生了一個皇帝外戚得權的成例。
   Translation: However, a precedent of the emperor's relatives gaining power has already been established in these military actions.
   Grammar Structure: This is a complex sentence with an adverbial clause of place "在這些軍事行動中" (in these military actions) and a main clause "已產生了一個皇帝外戚得權的成例" (a precedent of the emperor's relatives gaining power has already been established).
   Important Words:

   - 產生 (caan2 sang1): generate, produce

   - 外戚 (ngoi6 cik1): relatives by marriage

   - 成例 (sing4 lai6): precedent

2. 劉徹是一個意志堅強的人，他也深恐自己的權力落入他人之手。
   Translation: Liu Che is a person with a strong will, he also deeply fears his power falling into the hands of others.
   Grammar Structure: This is a compound sentence with two independent clauses. The first clause "劉徹是一個意志堅強的人" (Liu Che is a person with a strong will), and the second clause "他也深恐自己的權力落入他人之手" (he also deeply fears his power falling into the hands of others).

   Translation: But he was too harsh on others.
   Grammar Structure: The sentence is in the structure of "而对...则...过...". "而对..." indicates a contrast to the previous sentence, "则" indicates the condition or situation, and "过..." indicates the degree of the action.

   Translation: In short, during the process of campaigning against the Huns, he amassed great power, which could neither be institutionalized nor delegated.
   Grammar Structure: The sentence is in the structure of "总之，在...过程中...既...也...". "总之" indicates a summary or conclusion, "在...过程中" indicates the context or situation, and "既...也..." indicates two conditions or situations that are both true.

   Translation: Li Guang, as a capable general, won people's hearts.

   Grammar Structure: Time Phrase (兩年之後) + Subject (劉秀) + Verb (稱帝) + Transition Phrase (至此) + Noun Phrase (漢代「中興」).
   Important Words:
   - 兩年之後 (liang3 nian2 zhi1 hou4): two years later.
   - 劉秀 (Liu Xiu): A member of the Han dynasty royal family who restored the Han dynasty after the collapse of the short-lived Xin dynasty.
   - 稱帝 (cheng1 di4): verb, to proclaim oneself emperor.
   - 至此 (zhi4 ci3): until now, up to this point.
   - 漢代 (han4 dai4): Han dynasty.
   - 中興 (zhong1 xing1): revival, resurgence.

3. Sentence: 當時西安仍在農民軍手中，劉秀以洛陽為國都，他的旗幟全用紅色，以與「前漢」之黃色有別。
   Translation: At that time, Xi'an was still in the hands of the peasant army, Liu Xiu made Luoyang the capital, his flag was all red, to distinguish it from the yellow of the "Former Han".
   Grammar Structure: Time Phrase (當時) + Subject 1 (西安) + Verb Phrase 1 (仍在農民軍手中) + Comma + Subject 2 (劉秀) + Verb Phrase 2 (以洛陽為國都) + Comma + Subject 3 (他的旗幟) + Verb Phrase 3 (全用紅色) + Transition Phrase (以與) + Noun Phrase (「前漢」之黃色有別).

   - 當時 (dang1 shi2): at that time.

   - 旗幟 (qi2 zhi4): flag.

   Translation: [Introduction] After the brief chaos of Wang Mang's usurpation, Emperor Guangwu of the Eastern Han, Liu Xiu, revived the Han Empire under the circumstances of peasant uprisings and local warlords' separatism.

   Translation: In order to reconcile the conflicts of interests among all parties, so that they can coexist in harmony,
   Grammar Structure: This sentence is a complex sentence with two clauses. The first clause "為了調和各方的利害衝突" is a prepositional phrase indicating the purpose. The second clause "使彼此都能和諧並存" is a causative sentence.

   Translation: Finally, after the calamity of the Party's imprisonment, the conflicting parties pushed the Han Empire towards the fate of destruction.
   Grammar Structure: This sentence is a complex sentence with multiple clauses. It starts with an adverb "終於" (finally), followed by a prepositional phrase "在黨錮之禍後" (after the calamity of the Party's imprisonment) which sets the time context. The main clause is "衝突的各方將漢帝國推向敗亡的命運" (the conflicting parties pushed the Han Empire towards the fate of destruction), where "衝突的各方" is the subject, "將漢帝國推向敗亡的命運" is the predicate.

   Translation: The carvings on these bricks were originally for the deceased to appreciate.
   Grammar Structure: Subject + Verb + Object. This sentence uses the structure of "這些 (these) + noun + 上之 (on the) + noun + 原為 (originally for) + noun + 之用 (for use)".
   Important Words: 
   - 這些 (these): ze5 kei1
   - 磚石 (bricks): zyun1 sek6
   - 雕刻 (carvings): diu1 hak1

   - 欣賞 (appreciate): yan1 soeng6

2. Sentence: 它們埋在葬穴，面對棺槨
   Translation: They are buried in tombs, facing the coffin.

   Translation: Instead, they use historical events, strange legends, legendary figures, or daily life as themes.

2. 由畫像磚上可以看到，當時高層人士穿著長袖的袍服，普遍穿戴頭巾。

   Translation: Whether hosting a banquet, playing an instrument, or playing games and explaining history, all are done sitting on the ground.

3. 漁獵仍為高級人士消遣的場合，劇院不曾出現，可是以歌舞取樂卻又所在多有，富裕之家以雜耍者和魔術家相娛。
   Translation: Fishing and hunting are still occasions for the amusement of the upper class, theaters have not appeared, but there are many places where singing and dancing are enjoyed, and wealthy families entertain themselves with jugglers and magicians.

   - 魔術家 (mo1 seot6 gaa1): magician1. Sentence: 有些當日之演出在今日仍令人感到興味盎然。

   Translation: Some of the performances of that day still arouse interest today.

   Grammar Structure: The sentence uses the structure "有些...在...仍...". "有些" (some) is a quantifier, "當日之演出" (the performances of that day) is the subject, "在今日" (today) is the time, "仍" (still) is an adverb of time, and "令人感到興味盎然" (arouse interest) is the predicate.

   Important Words:
   - 有些 (jau1 se1): some
   - 當日 (dong1 jat6): that day
   - 演出 (jin2 ceot1): performance
   - 今日 (gam1 jat6): today
   - 仍 (jung4): still
   - 令人感到 (ling6 jan4 gam2 dou3): make people feel
   - 興味盎然 (hing1 mei6 ong1 jin4): interesting

2. Sentence: 一般常人工作時則穿著類似睡衣的寬鬆褐杉和犢鼻褲（短褲），偶爾還加一件及膝之短袍。

   Translation: Ordinary people usually wear loose brown shirts and shorts similar to pajamas when they work, and occasionally add a short robe that reaches the knee.

   Grammar Structure: The sentence uses the structure "一般...則...，偶爾還...". "一般" (usually) is an adverb of frequency, "常人工作時" (when ordinary people work) is the time, "則" (then) is a conjunction, "穿著類似睡衣的寬鬆褐杉和犢鼻褲（短褲）" (wear loose brown shirts and shorts similar to pajamas) is the predicate, and "偶爾還加一件及膝之短袍" (occasionally add a short robe that reaches the knee) is an additional action.

   Important Words:
   - 一般 (jat1 bun1): usually
   - 常人 (soeng4 jan4): ordinary people
   - 工作 (gung1 zok3): work
   - 穿著 (cyun1 zoek6): wear

   - 睡衣 (seoi6 ji1): pajamas

   Translation: About fifty years ago, a lacquerware was unearthed in a tomb in Korea, with the signatures of two artists on it, and the year marked, equivalent to the fourth year AD.

   - 公元四年 (gong1 yuan2 si4 nian2): the fourth year AD1. Sentence: 而外蒙古國都烏蘭巴托也有這兩位工匠署名的漆器出土，所署年份相當於公元前二年。
   Translation: Moreover, lacquerware signed by these two craftsmen has also been unearthed in Ulan Bator, the capital of Outer Mongolia, and the year of signature is equivalent to 2 BC.
   Grammar Structure: The sentence uses a complex structure with multiple clauses. It starts with the conjunction "而" (moreover), followed by the subject "外蒙古國都烏蘭巴托" (Ulan Bator, the capital of Outer Mongolia). The main verb "有" (has) is then used to introduce the object "這兩位工匠署名的漆器出土" (lacquerware signed by these two craftsmen unearthed). The last part of the sentence "所署年份相當於公元前二年" (the year of signature is equivalent to 2 BC) provides additional information about the object.
   Important Words:
   - 而 (ji4): and, moreover
   - 外蒙古國 (ngoi6 mung4 gu2 gwok3): Outer Mongolia
   - 烏蘭巴托 (wu1 laan4 baa1 tok3): Ulan Bator
   - 工匠 (gung1 zoeng6): craftsman
   - 署名 (syu3 ming4): sign one's name

   Translation: Therefore, every time this day comes, the bureaucrats of the Han Dynasty, including the central government and local officials, would change into red robes on time.
   Grammar Structure: This sentence is a complex sentence with multiple clauses. The main clause is "漢代的官僚，包括中央政府及地方官，便都按時換著紅色袍服", and it's preceded by the adverbial clause "因此，每逢這一天".
   Vocabulary:
   - 因此 (jan1 ci2): therefore
   - 每逢 (mui5 fung4): every time
   - 這一天 (ze2 jat1 tin1): this day
   - 漢代 (hon3 doi6): Han Dynasty
   - 官僚 (gun1 liu4): bureaucrats
   - 包括 (baau1 kut3): including
   - 中央政府 (zung1 joeng4 zing3 fu2): central government
   - 地方官 (dei6 fong1 gun1): local officials

   - 換 (wun6): change

   - 袍服 (pou4 fuk6): robes

   Translation: In the eyes of people at that time, it may be thought that participation has the effect of promoting.

2. 在漢代，尤其是後漢的國家祭典中包含以上種種複雜的成分，可見他們認為朝廷並不僅是人間的組織，如果再用它去維護某一社會階層的利益與特權，更是不成體統。
   Translation: In the Han Dynasty, especially in the national ceremonies of the Later Han, it contains various complex elements, showing that they believe that the court is not just an earthly organization, if it is used to maintain the interests and privileges of a certain social class, it is even more unseemly.
   Grammar Structure: The sentence is complex with multiple clauses. The main clause is "In the Han Dynasty", followed by several dependent clauses that provide additional information about the main clause.

   - 都 (all) [dōu]

   - 典籍 (classics) [dín jīk]1. Sentence: 由此看來，前述「自然宗教」、「國家祭典」都與妥協和保持原狀的宗旨相表裡。
   Translation: From this perspective, the aforementioned "natural religion" and "national ceremonies" are both in line with the purpose of compromise and maintaining the status quo.
   Grammar Structure: This sentence starts with an introductory phrase (由此看來), followed by the main subject (前述「自然宗教」、「國家祭典」). The verb (都與) connects the subject with the object (妥協和保持原狀的宗旨相表裡), forming a complete sentence.
   Important Words:
   - 由此看來 (jau4 ci2 hon3 loi4): from this perspective
   - 前述 (cin4 seot6): aforementioned
   - 自然宗教 (zi6 jin4 zung1 gaau1): natural religion
   - 國家祭典 (gwok3 gaa1 zai3 din2): national ceremonies
   - 妥協 (to3 hip3): compromise
   - 保持原狀 (bou2 ci4 jyun4 zong6): maintain the status quo

2. Sentence: 這種漢代的思想體系，劉秀和他的兒子劉莊都竭力提倡。
   Translation: This kind of ideological system of the Han Dynasty, Liu Xiu and his son Liu Zhuang both strongly advocated.
   Grammar Structure: This sentence starts with the subject (這種漢代的思想體系), followed by the main actors (劉秀和他的兒子劉莊). The verb (都竭力提倡) connects the actors with the subject, forming a complete sentence.
   Important Words:
   - 這種 (ze2 zung2): this kind

   - 兒子 (ji4 zi2): son
   - 劉莊 (lau4 zong1): Liu Zhuang (a person's name)
   - 竭力 (kit3 lik6): strongly
   - 提倡 (tai4 coeng4): advocate1. Sentence: 【豪強兼併是農村社會亂源】

   Translation: The combination of the powerful is the source of chaos in rural society.

   Grammar Structure: The sentence structure is Subject + Verb + Object. "豪強兼併" is the subject, "是" is the verb (is), and "農村社會亂源" is the object.

   Important Words:
   - 豪強 (hou4 koeng4): powerful

   - 社會 (se5 wui6*2): society
   - 亂源 (lyun6 jyun4): source of chaos

2. Sentence: 劉秀和劉莊在財政稅收上的表現也相當成功。

   Translation: Liu Xiu and Liu Zhuang were also quite successful in their financial and tax collection performance.

   Grammar Structure: The sentence structure is Subject + Location + Verb + Adjective. "劉秀和劉莊" is the subject, "在財政稅收上的表現" is the location (in the performance of financial and tax collection), "也" is the adverb (also), and "相當成功" is the adjective (quite successful).

   Important Words:
   - 劉秀 (lau4 sau3): Liu Xiu (a name)
   - 和 (wo4): and
   - 劉莊 (lau4 zong1): Liu Zhuang (a name)
   - 在 (zoi6): in
   - 財政 (coi4 zing3): finance

3. Sentence: 他們的方針是將稅率極度抑低，可是在規定的範圍內毫不通融地執行。

   Translation: Their policy is to keep the tax rate extremely low, but it is strictly enforced within the prescribed range.

   Grammar Structure: The sentence structure is Subject + Verb + Object + Conjunction + Adverb + Verb. "他們的方針" is the subject, "是將稅率極度抑低" is the verb phrase (is to keep the tax rate extremely low), "可是" is the conjunction (but), "在規定的範圍內" is the adverb (within the prescribed range), and "毫不通融地執行" is the verb phrase (strictly enforced).

   Important Words:

2. Sentence: 政府既無從以累進稅率抽稅，通常的情形便是稅收短絀，再則又要對貧弱無靠的人民周濟，也連帶受牽累。
   Translation: The government, unable to tax with a progressive tax rate, usually results in a shortfall in tax revenue. Furthermore, it has to aid the poor and helpless people, which also brings about related difficulties.

The second clause "通常的情形便是稅收短絀" is a subject-predicate-object structure, where "通常的情形" is the subject, "稅收短絀" is the object. The third clause "再則又要對貧弱無靠的人民周濟" is a subject-predicate-object structure, where "再則" is the subject, "對貧弱無靠的人民周濟" is the object. The fourth clause "也連帶受牽累" is a subject-predicate structure, where "也" is the subject and "連帶受牽累" is the predicate.

     - 無從 (mou4 cong4): unable to

     - 人民 (jan4 man4): people
